\"text\": \"In Apache Beam v2.62.0, the pipeline graph translation layer is split across two locations. The former 'runners/core-construction-java/' module has been merged into 'sdks/java/core/', while 'runners/core-java/' contains runner execution primitives.\\n\\n**runners/core-java/** -- Runner execution primitives:\\n- `runners/core-java/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/core/SplittableParDoViaKeyedWorkItems.java` (SplittableParDoViaKeyedWorkItems) -- Implements PTransformOverrideFactory to translate SplittableParDo into runner-executable keyed work items.\\n- `runners/core-java/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/core/construction/SerializablePipelineOptions.java` (SerializablePipelineOptions) -- Serializes pipeline options for the construction/translation layer.\\n\\n**TransformHierarchy walker** (now in sdks/java/core, formerly runners/core-construction-java):\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/TransformHierarchy.java` (TransformHierarchy) -- The central pipeline-graph walker. Maintains the tree of composite and primitive transforms, and exposes a visitor API (PipelineVisitor) used by all runner translators to traverse the DAG.\\n\\n**PTransformOverride mechanism**:\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverride.java` (PTransformOverride) -- Pairs a PTransformMatcher with a PTransformOverrideFactory; Pipeline.replaceAll() walks the hierarchy applying these overrides before translation.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverrideFactory.java` (PTransformOverrideFactory) -- Interface every runner-specific replacement factory must implement, producing a PTransformReplacement.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PTransformMatchers.java` (PTransformMatchers) -- Factory methods for common PTransformMatcher predicates (splittableParDo, classEqualTo, urnEqualTo, etc.).\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PTransformTranslation.java` (PTransformTranslation) -- Registry mapping PTransform subclasses to their RunnerApi URNs and payload translators.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PTransformReplacements.java` (PTransformReplacements) -- Helpers to build ReplacementOutput maps when wiring override outputs back to the graph.\\n\\n**PipelineTranslation** (Runner-API / proto serialization):\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PipelineTranslation.java` (PipelineTranslation) -- Converts a Java Pipeline object to/from the RunnerApi.Pipeline proto used by portable runners.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/SdkComponents.java` (SdkComponents) -- Accumulates all coders, windowing strategies, environments and transforms referenced during proto translation.\\n\\n**ExecutableStagePayload construction**:\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ExecutableStageTranslation.java` (ExecutableStageTranslation) -- Extracts an ExecutableStagePayload proto from an applied transform whose spec URN is the executable-stage URN.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ExecutableStage.java` (ExecutableStage) -- Interface for a fused group of transforms sharing an environment; toPTransform() serialises it to ExecutableStagePayload.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ImmutableExecutableStage.java` (ImmutableExecutableStage) -- Concrete immutable implementation of ExecutableStage.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/GreedyPipelineFuser.java` (GreedyPipelineFuser) -- Entry point: walks a QueryablePipeline and greedily fuses compatible transforms into ExecutableStages.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/GreedyStageFuser.java` (GreedyStageFuser) -- Fuses a single root transform with compatible downstream transforms into one ExecutableStage.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/FusedPipeline.java` (FusedPipeline) -- Result of pipeline fusion: a set of ExecutableStages plus runner-executed root transforms.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/QueryablePipeline.java` (QueryablePipeline) -- Wraps a RunnerApi.Pipeline and provides graph-query helpers used during fusion.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/PipelineValidator.java` (PipelineValidator) -- Validates proto pipeline structure, including ExecutableStagePayload consistency.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ProtoOverrides.java` (ProtoOverrides) -- Proto-level equivalent of PTransformOverride; replaces URN-matched transforms in the RunnerApi graph.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/SplittableParDoExpander.java` (SplittableParDoExpander) -- Expands splittable DoFns in the proto pipeline graph before fusion.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/SideInputReference.java` (SideInputReference) -- Models a side-input reference inside an ExecutableStagePayload.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/UserStateReference.java` (UserStateReference) -- Models a user-state reference inside an ExecutableStagePayload.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/TimerReference.java` (TimerReference) -- Models a timer reference inside an ExecutableStagePayload.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/PipelineNode.java` (PipelineNode) -- Typed node wrappers (PTransformNode, PCollectionNode, etc.) used in the proto graph representation.\\n\\n**BoundedSource / UnboundedSource adapter classes**:\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/UnboundedReadFromBoundedSource.java` (UnboundedReadFromBoundedSource / BoundedToUnboundedSourceAdapter) -- Wraps a BoundedSource as an UnboundedSource so it can be consumed by streaming runners; the primary bounded-to-unbounded source adapter in the construction layer.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ReadTranslation.java` (ReadTranslation) -- Translates Read.from(BoundedSource) and Read.from(UnboundedSource) to/from their RunnerApi representations, encoding source payloads for both source types.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/SplittableParDo.java` (SplittableParDo) -- OverrideFactory that replaces Read.from(BoundedSource/UnboundedSource) with a splittable DoFn-based primitive for portable execution.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":355,"cache_read_input_tokens":59192,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":355,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b9e18041-8486-4d48-ab47-a886cdd470b3","uuid":"ec5d91bd-354b-406b-a06a-d52d214c3c47"}

The former 'runners/core-construction-java/' module has been merged into 'sdks/java/core/', while 'runners/core-java/' contains runner execution primitives.\\n\\n**runners/core-java/** -- Runner execution primitives:\\n- `runners/core-java/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/core/SplittableParDoViaKeyedWorkItems.java` (SplittableParDoViaKeyedWorkItems) -- Implements PTransformOverrideFactory to translate SplittableParDo into runner-executable keyed work items.\\n- `runners/core-java/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/core/construction/SerializablePipelineOptions.java` (SerializablePipelineOptions) -- Serializes pipeline options for the construction/translation layer.\\n\\n**TransformHierarchy walker** (now in sdks/java/core, formerly runners/core-construction-java):\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/TransformHierarchy.java` (TransformHierarchy) -- The central pipeline-graph walker. Pipeline.replaceAll() walks the hierarchy applying these overrides before translation.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverrideFactory.java` (PTransformOverrideFactory) -- Interface every runner-specific replacement factory must implement, producing a PTransformReplacement.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PTransformMatchers.java` (PTransformMatchers) -- Factory methods for common PTransformMatcher predicates (splittableParDo, classEqualTo, urnEqualTo, etc.).\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PTransformTranslation.java` (PTransformTranslation) -- Registry mapping PTransform subclasses to their RunnerApi URNs and payload translators.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PTransformReplacements.java` (PTransformReplacements) -- Helpers to build ReplacementOutput maps when wiring override outputs back to the graph.\\n\\n**PipelineTranslation** (Runner-API / proto serialization):\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PipelineTranslation.java` (PipelineTranslation) -- Converts a Java Pipeline object to/from the RunnerApi.Pipeline proto used by portable runners.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/SdkComponents.java` (SdkComponents) -- Accumulates all coders, windowing strategies, environments and transforms referenced during proto translation.\\n\\n**ExecutableStagePayload construction**:\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ExecutableStageTranslation.java` (ExecutableStageTranslation) -- Extracts an ExecutableStagePayload proto from an applied transform whose spec URN is the executable-stage URN.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ExecutableStage.java` (ExecutableStage) -- Interface for a fused group of transforms sharing an environment; toPTransform() serialises it to ExecutableStagePayload.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ImmutableExecutableStage.java` (ImmutableExecutableStage) -- Concrete immutable implementation of ExecutableStage.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/GreedyPipelineFuser.java` (GreedyPipelineFuser) -- Entry point: walks a QueryablePipeline and greedily fuses compatible transforms into ExecutableStages.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/GreedyStageFuser.java` (GreedyStageFuser) -- Fuses a single root transform with compatible downstream transforms into one ExecutableStage.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/FusedPipeline.java` (FusedPipeline) -- Result of pipeline fusion: a set of ExecutableStages plus runner-executed root transforms.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/QueryablePipeline.java` (QueryablePipeline) -- Wraps a RunnerApi.Pipeline and provides graph-query helpers used during fusion.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/PipelineValidator.java` (PipelineValidator) -- Validates proto pipeline structure, including ExecutableStagePayload consistency.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ProtoOverrides.java` (ProtoOverrides) -- Proto-level equivalent of PTransformOverride; the primary bounded-to-unbounded source adapter in the construction layer.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ReadTranslation.java` (ReadTranslation) -- Translates Read.from(BoundedSource) and Read.from(UnboundedSource) to/from their RunnerApi representations, encoding source payloads for both source types.\\n- `sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/SplittableParDo.java` (SplittableParDo) -- OverrideFactory that replaces Read.from(BoundedSource/UnboundedSource) with a splittable DoFn-based primitive for portable execution.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
